<s> falder bows his head <\s>
<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>

<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>
<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>
<s> it couldn't have been four minutes sir because i ran all the way <\s>
<s> during those four minutes you say you remember nothing <\s>
<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>
<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>
<s> your husband was not under the influence of liquor then <\s>
<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>
<s> my dress was torn and i was half choking <\s>
<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>
<s> did he ever give you any money <\s>
<s> to buy an outfit for me and the children and get all ready to start <\s>
<s> did that surprise you or not <\s>
<s> that he had money to give you <\s>
<s> yes because on the morning when my husband nearly killed me my friend cried because he hadn't the money to get me away <\s>
<s> he told me afterwards he'd come into a windfall <\s>
<s> and when did you last see him <\s>
<s> the day he was taken away sir <\s>
<s> it was the day we were to have started <\s>
<s> oh yes the morning of the arrest <\s>
<s> well did you see him at all between the friday and that morning <\s>
<s> ruth nods what was his manner then <\s>
<s> dumb like sometimes he didn't seem able to say a word <\s>
<s> as if something unusual had happened to him <\s>
<s> painful or pleasant or what <\s>
<s> like a fate hanging over him <\s>
<s> hesitating tell me did you love the prisoner very much <\s>

<s> and had he a very great affection for you <\s>
<s> looking at falder yes sir <\s>
<s> now ma'am do you or do you not think that your danger and unhappiness would seriously affect his balance his control over his actions <\s>
<s> for a moment like i think it would <\s>
<s> was he very much upset that friday morning or was he fairly calm <\s>
<s> i could hardly bear to let him go from me <\s>
<s> do you still love him <\s>
<s> with her eyes on falder he's ruined himself for me <\s>
<s> ruth remains stoically upright in the witness box <\s>
<s> in a considerate voice when you left him on the morning of friday the 7th you would not say that he was out of his mind i suppose <\s>
<s> thank you i've no further questions to ask you <\s>
<s> bending a little forward to the jury i would have done the same for him i would indeed <\s>

<s> faults on both sides <\s>

<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>

<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>

<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>
<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>
<s> it couldn't have been four minutes sir because i ran all the way <\s>
<s> during those four minutes you say you remember nothing <\s>
<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>
<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>
<s> your husband was not under the influence of liquor then <\s>
<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>

<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>
<s> did he ever give you any money <\s>

<s> that he had money to give you <\s>

<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>

<s> to falder you admit altering this cheque <\s>
<s> falder bows his head <\s>
<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>
<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>
<s> it couldn't have been four minutes sir because i ran all the way <\s>
<s> during those four minutes you say you remember nothing <\s>
<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>
<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>
<s> your husband was not under the influence of liquor then <\s>
<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>
<s> my dress was torn and i was half choking <\s>
<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>
<s> did he ever give you any money <\s>
<s> to buy an outfit for me and the children and get all ready to start <\s>
<s> did that surprise you or not <\s>
<s> that he had money to give you <\s>
<s> yes because on the morning when my husband nearly killed me my friend cried because he hadn't the money to get me away <\s>
<s> he told me afterwards he'd come into a windfall <\s>
<s> and when did you last see him <\s>
<s> the day he was taken away sir <\s>

<s> painful or pleasant or what <\s>

<s> i couldn't help it your lordship <\s>
<s> i didn't seem able to <\s>
<s> the judge slightly shrugs his shoulders <\s>
<s> how did you come to know her <\s>
<s> through my married sister <\s>
<s> did you know whether she was happy with her husband <\s>
<s> it was trouble all the time <\s>
<s> you knew her husband <\s>
<s> only through her he's a brute <\s>
<s> i can't allow indiscriminate abuse of a person not present <\s>
<s> bowing if your lordship pleases <\s>
<s> to falder you admit altering this cheque <\s>
<s> falder bows his head <\s>
<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>
<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>
<s> it couldn't have been four minutes sir because i ran all the way <\s>
<s> during those four minutes you say you remember nothing <\s>
<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>
<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>
<s> your husband was not under the influence of liquor then <\s>
<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>
<s> my dress was torn and i was half choking <\s>
<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>
<s> did he ever give you any money <\s>
<s> to buy an outfit for me and the children and get all ready to start <\s>
<s> did that surprise you or not <\s>
<s> that he had money to give you <\s>
<s> yes because on the morning when my husband nearly killed me my friend cried because he hadn't the money to get me away <\s>
<s> he told me afterwards he'd come into a windfall <\s>
<s> and when did you last see him <\s>
<s> the day he was taken away sir <\s>
<s> it was the day we were to have started <\s>
<s> oh yes the morning of the arrest <\s>
<s> well did you see him at all between the friday and that morning <\s>
<s> ruth nods what was his manner then <\s>
<s> dumb like sometimes he didn't seem able to say a word <\s>
<s> as if something unusual had happened to him <\s>
<s> painful or pleasant or what <\s>
<s> like a fate hanging over him <\s>

<s> and had he a very great affection for you <\s>
<s> looking at falder yes sir <\s>
<s> now ma'am do you or do you not think that your danger and unhappiness would seriously affect his balance his control over his actions <\s>
<s> for a moment like i think it would <\s>
<s> was he very much upset that friday morning or was he fairly calm <\s>

<s> with her eyes on falder he's ruined himself for me <\s>

<s> i call the prisoner my lord <\s>
<s> falder leaves the dock goes into the witness box and is duly sworn <\s>
<s> what is your name <\s>
<s> you are not married <\s>
<s> falder shakes his head frome <\s>
<s> how long have you known the last witness <\s>
<s> is her account of the relationship between you a correct one <\s>
<s> you became devotedly attached to her however <\s>
<s> though you knew she was a married woman <\s>
<s> i couldn't help it your lordship <\s>
<s> i didn't seem able to <\s>
<s> the judge slightly shrugs his shoulders <\s>
<s> how did you come to know her <\s>
<s> through my married sister <\s>
<s> did you know whether she was happy with her husband <\s>
<s> it was trouble all the time <\s>
<s> you knew her husband <\s>
<s> only through her he's a brute <\s>
<s> i can't allow indiscriminate abuse of a person not present <\s>
<s> bowing if your lordship pleases <\s>
<s> to falder you admit altering this cheque <\s>
<s> falder bows his head <\s>
<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>
<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>
<s> it couldn't have been four minutes sir because i ran all the way <\s>
<s> during those four minutes you say you remember nothing <\s>
<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>
<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>
<s> your husband was not under the influence of liquor then <\s>
<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>
<s> my dress was torn and i was half choking <\s>
<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>
<s> did he ever give you any money <\s>
<s> to buy an outfit for me and the children and get all ready to start <\s>
<s> did that surprise you or not <\s>
<s> that he had money to give you <\s>
<s> yes because on the morning when my husband nearly killed me my friend cried because he hadn't the money to get me away <\s>
<s> he told me afterwards he'd come into a windfall <\s>
<s> and when did you last see him <\s>
<s> the day he was taken away sir <\s>
<s> it was the day we were to have started <\s>
<s> oh yes the morning of the arrest <\s>
<s> well did you see him at all between the friday and that morning <\s>
<s> ruth nods what was his manner then <\s>
<s> dumb like sometimes he didn't seem able to say a word <\s>
<s> as if something unusual had happened to him <\s>
<s> painful or pleasant or what <\s>
<s> like a fate hanging over him <\s>
<s> hesitating tell me did you love the prisoner very much <\s>
<s> bowing her head yes <\s>
<s> and had he a very great affection for you <\s>
<s> looking at falder yes sir <\s>
<s> now ma'am do you or do you not think that your danger and unhappiness would seriously affect his balance his control over his actions <\s>
<s> for a moment like i think it would <\s>
<s> was he very much upset that friday morning or was he fairly calm <\s>
<s> i could hardly bear to let him go from me <\s>
<s> do you still love him <\s>
<s> with her eyes on falder he's ruined himself for me <\s>
<s> ruth remains stoically upright in the witness box <\s>
<s> in a considerate voice when you left him on the morning of friday the 7th you would not say that he was out of his mind i suppose <\s>
<s> thank you i've no further questions to ask you <\s>

<s> though you knew she was a married woman <\s>

<s> how did you come to know her <\s>
<s> through my married sister <\s>
<s> did you know whether she was happy with her husband <\s>
<s> it was trouble all the time <\s>

<s> to falder you admit altering this cheque <\s>
<s> falder bows his head <\s>
<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>
<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>
<s> it couldn't have been four minutes sir because i ran all the way <\s>
<s> during those four minutes you say you remember nothing <\s>
<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>
<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>
<s> your husband was not under the influence of liquor then <\s>
<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>
<s> my dress was torn and i was half choking <\s>
<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>
<s> did he ever give you any money <\s>
<s> to buy an outfit for me and the children and get all ready to start <\s>
<s> did that surprise you or not <\s>
<s> that he had money to give you <\s>
<s> yes because on the morning when my husband nearly killed me my friend cried because he hadn't the money to get me away <\s>
<s> he told me afterwards he'd come into a windfall <\s>
<s> and when did you last see him <\s>
<s> the day he was taken away sir <\s>

<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>

<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>

<s> painful or pleasant or what <\s>

<s> for a moment like i think it would <\s>

<s> i could hardly bear to let him go from me <\s>
<s> do you still love him <\s>
<s> with her eyes on falder he's ruined himself for me <\s>
<s> ruth remains stoically upright in the witness box <\s>
<s> in a considerate voice when you left him on the morning of friday the 7th you would not say that he was out of his mind i suppose <\s>
<s> thank you i've no further questions to ask you <\s>
<s> bending a little forward to the jury i would have done the same for him i would indeed <\s>

<s> how did you come to know her <\s>
<s> through my married sister <\s>

<s> to falder you admit altering this cheque <\s>
<s> falder bows his head <\s>
<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>

<s> my dress was torn and i was half choking <\s>
<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>
<s> did he ever give you any money <\s>
<s> to buy an outfit for me and the children and get all ready to start <\s>
<s> did that surprise you or not <\s>
<s> that he had money to give you <\s>
<s> yes because on the morning when my husband nearly killed me my friend cried because he hadn't the money to get me away <\s>
<s> he told me afterwards he'd come into a windfall <\s>
<s> and when did you last see him <\s>
<s> the day he was taken away sir <\s>
<s> it was the day we were to have started <\s>
<s> oh yes the morning of the arrest <\s>
<s> well did you see him at all between the friday and that morning <\s>
<s> ruth nods what was his manner then <\s>
<s> dumb like sometimes he didn't seem able to say a word <\s>
<s> as if something unusual had happened to him <\s>
<s> painful or pleasant or what <\s>
<s> like a fate hanging over him <\s>
<s> hesitating tell me did you love the prisoner very much <\s>
<s> bowing her head yes <\s>
<s> and had he a very great affection for you <\s>
<s> looking at falder yes sir <\s>
<s> now ma'am do you or do you not think that your danger and unhappiness would seriously affect his balance his control over his actions <\s>
<s> for a moment like i think it would <\s>
<s> was he very much upset that friday morning or was he fairly calm <\s>
<s> i could hardly bear to let him go from me <\s>
<s> do you still love him <\s>
<s> with her eyes on falder he's ruined himself for me <\s>
<s> ruth remains stoically upright in the witness box <\s>
<s> in a considerate voice when you left him on the morning of friday the 7th you would not say that he was out of his mind i suppose <\s>
<s> thank you i've no further questions to ask you <\s>
<s> bending a little forward to the jury i would have done the same for him i would indeed <\s>
<s> you say your married life is an unhappy one <\s>
<s> faults on both sides <\s>
<s> only that i never bowed down to him <\s>
<s> i don't see why i should sir not to a man like that <\s>
<s> you refused to obey him <\s>
<s> avoiding the question i've always studied him to keep things nice <\s>
<s> until you met the prisoner was that it <\s>
<s> no even after that <\s>
<s> i ask you know because you seem to me to glory in this affection of yours for the prisoner <\s>
<s> it's the only thing in my life now <\s>
<s> staring at her hard well step down please <\s>
<s> ruth looks at falder then passes quietly down and takes her seat among the witnesses <\s>
<s> i call the prisoner my lord <\s>
<s> falder leaves the dock goes into the witness box and is duly sworn <\s>
<s> what is your name <\s>
<s> you are not married <\s>
<s> falder shakes his head frome <\s>
<s> how long have you known the last witness <\s>
<s> is her account of the relationship between you a correct one <\s>
<s> you became devotedly attached to her however <\s>
<s> though you knew she was a married woman <\s>
<s> i couldn't help it your lordship <\s>
<s> i didn't seem able to <\s>
<s> the judge slightly shrugs his shoulders <\s>
<s> how did you come to know her <\s>
<s> through my married sister <\s>
<s> did you know whether she was happy with her husband <\s>
<s> it was trouble all the time <\s>
<s> you knew her husband <\s>
<s> only through her he's a brute <\s>
<s> i can't allow indiscriminate abuse of a person not present <\s>
<s> bowing if your lordship pleases <\s>
<s> to falder you admit altering this cheque <\s>
<s> falder bows his head <\s>
<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>

<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>
<s> it couldn't have been four minutes sir because i ran all the way <\s>
<s> during those four minutes you say you remember nothing <\s>
<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>
<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>
<s> your husband was not under the influence of liquor then <\s>
<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>
<s> my dress was torn and i was half choking <\s>
<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>
<s> did he ever give you any money <\s>
<s> to buy an outfit for me and the children and get all ready to start <\s>
<s> did that surprise you or not <\s>
<s> that he had money to give you <\s>
<s> yes because on the morning when my husband nearly killed me my friend cried because he hadn't the money to get me away <\s>
<s> he told me afterwards he'd come into a windfall <\s>
<s> and when did you last see him <\s>
<s> the day he was taken away sir <\s>
<s> it was the day we were to have started <\s>
<s> oh yes the morning of the arrest <\s>
<s> well did you see him at all between the friday and that morning <\s>
<s> ruth nods what was his manner then <\s>
<s> dumb like sometimes he didn't seem able to say a word <\s>
<s> as if something unusual had happened to him <\s>
<s> painful or pleasant or what <\s>
<s> like a fate hanging over him <\s>
<s> hesitating tell me did you love the prisoner very much <\s>
<s> bowing her head yes <\s>
<s> and had he a very great affection for you <\s>
<s> looking at falder yes sir <\s>
<s> now ma'am do you or do you not think that your danger and unhappiness would seriously affect his balance his control over his actions <\s>
<s> for a moment like i think it would <\s>
<s> was he very much upset that friday morning or was he fairly calm <\s>
<s> i could hardly bear to let him go from me <\s>
<s> do you still love him <\s>
<s> with her eyes on falder he's ruined himself for me <\s>
<s> ruth remains stoically upright in the witness box <\s>
<s> in a considerate voice when you left him on the morning of friday the 7th you would not say that he was out of his mind i suppose <\s>
<s> thank you i've no further questions to ask you <\s>
<s> bending a little forward to the jury i would have done the same for him i would indeed <\s>
<s> you say your married life is an unhappy one <\s>
<s> faults on both sides <\s>
<s> only that i never bowed down to him <\s>
<s> i don't see why i should sir not to a man like that <\s>
<s> you refused to obey him <\s>
<s> avoiding the question i've always studied him to keep things nice <\s>
<s> until you met the prisoner was that it <\s>
<s> no even after that <\s>
<s> i ask you know because you seem to me to glory in this affection of yours for the prisoner <\s>
<s> it's the only thing in my life now <\s>
<s> staring at her hard well step down please <\s>
<s> ruth looks at falder then passes quietly down and takes her seat among the witnesses <\s>
<s> i call the prisoner my lord <\s>
<s> falder leaves the dock goes into the witness box and is duly sworn <\s>
<s> what is your name <\s>
<s> you are not married <\s>
<s> falder shakes his head frome <\s>
<s> how long have you known the last witness <\s>
<s> is her account of the relationship between you a correct one <\s>
<s> you became devotedly attached to her however <\s>
<s> though you knew she was a married woman <\s>
<s> i couldn't help it your lordship <\s>
<s> i didn't seem able to <\s>
<s> the judge slightly shrugs his shoulders <\s>
<s> how did you come to know her <\s>
<s> through my married sister <\s>
<s> did you know whether she was happy with her husband <\s>
<s> it was trouble all the time <\s>
<s> you knew her husband <\s>
<s> only through her he's a brute <\s>
<s> i can't allow indiscriminate abuse of a person not present <\s>
<s> bowing if your lordship pleases <\s>
<s> to falder you admit altering this cheque <\s>
<s> falder bows his head <\s>
<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>

<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>
<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>

<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>

<s> it wasn't always that <\s>

<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>

<s> that he had money to give you <\s>

<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>
<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>
<s> it couldn't have been four minutes sir because i ran all the way <\s>
<s> during those four minutes you say you remember nothing <\s>
<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>
<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>
<s> your husband was not under the influence of liquor then <\s>
<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>

<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>

<s> that he had money to give you <\s>

<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>
<s> falder is silent twisting his hands before him <\s>
<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>
<s> not more than fifty yards sir <\s>
<s> from the time davis went out to lunch to the time you cashed the cheque how long do you say it must have been <\s>
<s> it couldn't have been four minutes sir because i ran all the way <\s>
<s> during those four minutes you say you remember nothing <\s>
<s> yes i just managed to get away from him <\s>
<s> i went straight to my friend <\s>
<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>
<s> your husband was not under the influence of liquor then <\s>
<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>
<s> my dress was torn and i was half choking <\s>
<s> did you tell your friend what had happened <\s>
<s> i wish i never had <\s>
<s> did he ever speak to you about a cheque <\s>
<s> did he ever give you any money <\s>
<s> to buy an outfit for me and the children and get all ready to start <\s>
<s> did that surprise you or not <\s>
<s> that he had money to give you <\s>
<s> yes because on the morning when my husband nearly killed me my friend cried because he hadn't the money to get me away <\s>
<s> he told me afterwards he'd come into a windfall <\s>
<s> and when did you last see him <\s>
<s> the day he was taken away sir <\s>
<s> it was the day we were to have started <\s>
<s> oh yes the morning of the arrest <\s>
<s> well did you see him at all between the friday and that morning <\s>
<s> ruth nods what was his manner then <\s>
<s> dumb like sometimes he didn't seem able to say a word <\s>
<s> as if something unusual had happened to him <\s>
<s> painful or pleasant or what <\s>
<s> like a fate hanging over him <\s>
<s> hesitating tell me did you love the prisoner very much <\s>

<s> and had he a very great affection for you <\s>
<s> looking at falder yes sir <\s>
<s> now ma'am do you or do you not think that your danger and unhappiness would seriously affect his balance his control over his actions <\s>
<s> for a moment like i think it would <\s>
<s> was he very much upset that friday morning or was he fairly calm <\s>
<s> i could hardly bear to let him go from me <\s>
<s> do you still love him <\s>
<s> with her eyes on falder he's ruined himself for me <\s>
<s> ruth remains stoically upright in the witness box <\s>
<s> in a considerate voice when you left him on the morning of friday the 7th you would not say that he was out of his mind i suppose <\s>
<s> thank you i've no further questions to ask you <\s>

<s> falder bows his head <\s>
<s> carry your mind please to the morning of friday july the 7th and tell the jury what happened <\s>
<s> turning to the jury i was having my breakfast when she came <\s>
<s> her dress was all torn and she was gasping and couldn't seem to get her breath at all there were the marks of his fingers round her throat her arm was bruised and the blood had got into her eyes dreadfully <\s>
<s> it frightened me and then when she told me i felt i felt well it was too much for me <\s>
<s> hardening suddenly if you'd seen it having the feelings for her that i had you'd have felt the same i know <\s>
<s> when she left me because i had to go to the office i was out of my senses for fear that he'd do it again and thinking what i could do <\s>
<s> i couldn't work all the morning i was like that simply couldn't fix my mind on anything <\s>
<s> i couldn't think at all <\s>
<s> i seemed to have to keep moving <\s>
<s> when davis the other clerk gave me the cheque he said it'll do you good will to have a run with this <\s>
<s> you seem half off your chump this morning <\s>
<s> then when i had it in my hand i don't know how it came but it just flashed across me that if i put the ty and the nought there would be the money to get her away <\s>
<s> it just came and went i never thought of it again <\s>
<s> then davis went out to his luncheon and i don't really remember what i did till i'd pushed the cheque through to the cashier under the rail <\s>
<s> i remember his saying gold or notes <\s>
<s> then i suppose i knew what i'd done <\s>
<s> anyway when i got outside i wanted to chuck myself under a bus i wanted to throw the money away but it seemed i was in for it so i thought at any rate i'd save her <\s>
<s> of course the tickets i took for the passage and the little i gave her's been wasted and all except what i was obliged to spend myself i've restored <\s>
<s> i keep thinking over and over however it was i came to do it and how i can't have it all again to do differently <\s>

<s> how far is it from your office to the bank <\s>

<s> it was eight o'clock <\s>

<s> it wasn't always that <\s>
<s> in what condition were you <\s>
<s> in very bad condition sir <\s>

<s> i wish i never had <\s>

<s> that he had money to give you <\s>
<s> yes because on the morning when my husband nearly killed me my friend cried because he hadn't the money to get me away <\s>
<s> he told me afterwards he'd come into a windfall <\s>
<s> and when did you last see him <\s>

<s> i could hardly bear to let him go from me <\s>
